## Diagram 2

sequenceDiagram

## Diagram 3

```mermaid
flowchart TD
Start([Start]) --> CheckGlob{Is incoming code globally blacklisted?}
CheckGlob -->|Yes| NoUpdate1([Do not update last_status])
CheckGlob -->|No| CheckLast{Is code blacklisted for updating last_status?}
CheckLast -->|Yes| NoUpdate2([Do not update last_status])
CheckLast -->|No| CheckDealer{Is code blacklisted for dealers only?}
CheckDealer -->|Yes| DealerPath([Possibly update dealerLastStatusUpdate only])
CheckDealer -->|No| Update([Call update_entity_last_status and write last_status_update])
NoUpdate1 --> End([End])
NoUpdate2 --> End
DealerPath --> Update
Update --> End
```
